		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

		"ItemShopTags"					"consumable"
		"ItemQuality"					"consumable"
		"ItemShareability"				"ITEM_FULLY_SHAREABLE"
		"ItemStackable"					"0"
		"ItemPermanent"					"1"
		"ItemDroppable"               	"1"
		"ItemAliases"					"quicktype"
		"ItemDisassembleRule"			"DOTA_ITEM_DISASSEMBLE_NEVER"

	//raw meat eating channel - use this ability when eating raw meat
	"ability_item_eat_meat_raw"
	{
		// General
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"BaseClass"						"ability_datadriven"
		"AbilityBehavior"				"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_NO_TARGET | DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_CHANNELLED"
		"AbilityTextureName"			"life_stealer_open_wounds"
		
		// Casting
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityCastPoint"				"0.0"
		"AbilityCastAnimation"			"ACT_DOTA_CHANNEL_ABILITY_4"

		// Time		
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityChannelTime"			"2.0"
		"AbilityCooldown"				"0"

		// Cost
		//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
		"AbilityManaCost"				"0"
		
		"OnSpellStart"
		{
			"ApplyModifier"
			{
				"Target"			"CASTER"
				"ModifierName"		"modifier_eat_meat_raw"
			}
		}
		
		"OnAbilityEndChannel"
		{
			"RemoveModifier"
			{
				"Target"			"CASTER"
				"ModifierName"		"modifier_eat_meat_raw"
			}
			"RemoveAbility"
			{
				"Target"			"CASTER"
				"AbilityName"		"ability_item_eat_meat_raw"
			}
		}
		"OnChannelFinish"
		{
			"RemoveModifier"
			{
				"Target"			"CASTER"
				"ModifierName"		"modifier_eat_meat_raw"
			}				
			"RemoveAbility"
			{
				"Target"			"CASTER"
				"AbilityName"		"ability_item_eat_meat_raw"
			}
		}
		
		"Modifiers"
		{
			"modifier_eat_meat_raw"
			{					
				"ThinkInterval"			".2"
				"OnIntervalThink"
				{
					"Heal"
					{
						"Target"		"CASTER"
						"HealAmount"	"1"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
